" inke kaaran desh ke karodon logon ko dukh sahan karnaa padataa he

 " The Prime Minister indicated to extend the duration of 50 days and said that "after December 30, the suffering of honest people will reduce and the suffering of dishonest people will increase

 sarkaar badal chuki he

 nae sadasyon par samjhauta beete shuukravaar ko tazakastan ke dushambe main essio ke 14wein shikhar sammelan ke dauraan paarit ek kanoonee dastavej main aayaa
 Significantly, the SCO group currently consists of China, Kazakhstan, Kyrgyzstan, Russia, Tajikistan and Uzbekistan, while Afghanistan, India, Iran, Mongolia and Pakistan are observers and Belarus, Turkey and Sri Lanka are negotiating partners
 bharat ne ahmedabad ke motera stadium main pakistan ko duusare twanti-20 mukaable main 11 ranon se haraakar do maichon kii shrunkhlaa baraabar kar lee
 Chasing the target given by India, the Pakistan cricket team could only manage 181 runs in the loss of seven wickets in the prescribed 20 overs
 match main 59 gendon par tabadatod 72 ran banane evam ek wicket jhatakane ke kaaran yuvaraj singh ko main of da match evam shrunkhlaa main shandaar ballebaaji ke kaaran pakistani captain mohammad hafeez ko main of da siries chunaa gaya
 India's most successful bowler Ashok Dinda took three wickets
 pakistan kii taraf se hafeez ne teen chhakkon evam chah chaukon kii madad se sarvaadhik 55 ran (26 gend) banaae
 The Pakistani innings were started by Nasir Jamshed and Ahmed Shehzad
 jamshed 32 gendon par chaar chaukon or ek chakke kii madad se 41 ran banaakar out hue
 His wicket was taken by Ravichandran Ashwin
 shahzad 31 ran ke nijee yoga par yuvaraj singh kii gend par mahendra singh dhoni dwaara stump out ho gaye
 Shahzad hit three fours and a six off 29 balls
 umr akmal 24 ke nijee yoga par dinda kii gend par bold ho gaye
 After this, Shahid Afridi landed only 11 runs off five balls
 vah bhubaneshwar kumaar kii gend par rohit sharma ke haathon lapke gaye
 Hafeez catches Raina off Dinda
 kamran akmal paanch ran bana sake or dinda kii gend par kohli dwaara kaich out hue
 Umar Gul was caught by Ishant Sharma at the hands of Ajinkya Rahane
 shoeb malik teen ran par naabad laute
 For India, Dinda struck three, Bhuvneshwar Kumar, Sharma and Yuvraj took one wicket each
 isse pehle, yuvaraj singh (72) kii tufaani pari kii badaulat bhartiya team ne pakistan ke saamne 193 ranon kaa lakshya rakhaa
 Batting first after losing the toss, the Indian team scored 192 for five wickets in the scheduled 20 overs
 yuvaraj ne apni 36 gendon kii pari main chaar chauke or saat chakke lagaae
 India lost five wickets in the form of Ajinkya Rahane, Gautam Gambhir, Virat Kohli, Mahendra Singh Dhoni and Yuvraj
 gambheer ne 21 ran banaae jabaki rahane 28 ran banaakar out hue
 Rahane hit four fours off 26 balls while Gambhir hit four fours off 11 balls
 kohli ne 22 gendon par teen chaukon kii madad se 27 ranon kaa yogadan diya
 Rahane and Gambhir added 44 runs for the first wicket while 35 runs were added for the third wicket between Yuvraj and Kohli
 tippaniyan After this, Yuvraj and captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni added 97 runs for the fourth wicket
 dhoni ne apni 23 gendon kii pari main chaar chaukon kii madad se 33 ran banaae
 Umar Gul took four wickets for 37 runs
 bengaluru main khele gaye pehle match main pakistan ne bharat par kaaphi aasaan jeet hasil kii thi
 After bowling out India on a relatively low score, the Pakistani batsmen recovered from the initial setback to win by five wickets
